## 1. Introduction to Resource Controller

Laravel এ **Resource Controller** হলো এমন একটি controller structure, যেটা CRUD operation handle করার জন্য তৈরি করা হয়েছে।

CRUD মানে:

- **C** = Create
- **R** = Read
- **U** = Update
- **D** = Delete

Laravel বুঝে যে, বেশিরভাগ application-এ আমাদের data create, view, update, delete করার দরকার হয়। তাই Laravel একটি standard pattern দিয়েছে, যার নাম **Resource Controller**। 🎯

---

## 2. Why Resource Controller is Important

Resource Controller গুরুত্বপূর্ণ কারণ:

- CRUD operation standard way-তে organize করা যায়
- method naming convention clear থাকে
- route setup সহজ হয়
- বড় project-এ maintain করা সহজ হয়
- Laravel convention follow করা হয়

যদি manually route ও method লিখেন, তাহলে বেশি code লিখতে হয়। কিন্তু Resource Controller use করলে অনেক কিছু clean হয়ে যায়।

---

## 3. CRUD Concept and Resource Controller

ধরি, আপনি একটি **Student Management System** বানাচ্ছেন।

আপনার দরকার হবে:

- সব student list দেখা
- নতুন student add করা
- একটি specific student দেখা
- existing student edit করা
- student delete করা

এই ৫–৭ ধরনের কাজই Resource Controller handle করে।

---

## 4. How to Create a Resource Controller

Resource controller তৈরি করার command:

```bash
php artisan make:controller StudentController --resource
```

এতে Laravel একটি controller file তৈরি করবে, যেখানে CRUD related সব method skeleton আকারে থাকবে।

---

## 5. Generated Methods in Resource Controller

এই command চালালে সাধারণত নিচের methods পাওয়া যায়:

```php
public function index() {}
public function create() {}
public function store(Request $request) {}
public function show(string $id) {}
public function edit(string $id) {}
public function update(Request $request, string $id) {}
public function destroy(string $id) {}
```

এগুলোর কাজ:

- `index()` → সব record show করা
- `create()` → add form show করা
- `store()` → নতুন record save করা
- `show()` → single record show করা
- `edit()` → edit form show করা
- `update()` → edited data save করা
- `destroy()` → record delete করা

---

## 6. Route Resource

Resource controller-এর সবচেয়ে সুন্দর অংশ হলো route এক লাইনে define করা যায়।

```php
use App\Http\Controllers\StudentController;

Route::resource('students', StudentController::class);
```

এখন Laravel automatically সব CRUD route তৈরি করে দেবে। 🎉

---

## 7. Resource Routes Mapping Table

`Route::resource('students', StudentController::class);` লিখলে সাধারণত এই route গুলো তৈরি হয়:

| HTTP Method | URL                        | Controller Method | Purpose               |
| ----------- | -------------------------- | ----------------- | --------------------- |
| GET         | `/students`                | `index()`         | সব students দেখানো    |
| GET         | `/students/create`         | `create()`        | add form দেখানো       |
| POST        | `/students`                | `store()`         | নতুন student save করা |
| GET         | `/students/{student}`      | `show()`          | single student দেখানো |
| GET         | `/students/{student}/edit` | `edit()`          | edit form দেখানো      |
| PUT/PATCH   | `/students/{student}`      | `update()`        | student update করা    |
| DELETE      | `/students/{student}`      | `destroy()`       | student delete করা    |

এখানে convention follow করা হচ্ছে। তাই code বুঝতে সহজ হয়।

---

## 8. Full CRUD Project Idea

এখন আমরা একটি simple **Student CRUD Project** imagine করি।

Student table-এ থাকবে:

- id
- name
- email
- course
- timestamps

আমরা যা বানাবো:

- student list page
- add student form
- save student
- show single student
- edit student
- update student
- delete student

---

## 9. Creating Model, Migration, and Resource Controller

সব একসাথে create করতে পারেন:

```bash
php artisan make:model Student -mcr
```

এখানে:

- `-m` = migration তৈরি করবে
- `-c` = controller তৈরি করবে
- `-r` = resource controller তৈরি করবে

এতে আপনি এক command-এ তিনটি জিনিস পেয়ে যাবেন:

- `app/Models/Student.php`
- migration file
- `app/Http/Controllers/StudentController.php`

---

## 10. Database Migration Setup

ধরি migration file এ এই code লিখলেন:

```php
use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('students', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->string('name');
            $table->string('email');
            $table->string('course');
            $table->timestamps();
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('students');
    }
};
```

### এখানে কী হচ্ছে?

- `id()` → primary key
- `name` → student name
- `email` → student email
- `course` → course name
- `timestamps()` → `created_at` এবং `updated_at`

---

## 11. Running Migration

Database table create করার জন্য:

```bash
php artisan migrate
```

এখন database-এ `students` table তৈরি হয়ে যাবে।

---

## 12. Resource Controller Code

এখন একটি full resource controller code দেখি:

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use App\Models\Student;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class StudentController extends Controller
{
    public function index()
    {
        $students = Student::latest()->get();
        return view('students.index', compact('students'));
    }

    public function create()
    {
        return view('students.create');
    }

    public function store(Request $request)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'name'   => 'required',
            'email'  => 'required|email',
            'course' => 'required',
        ]);

        Student::create([
            'name'   => $request->name,
            'email'  => $request->email,
            'course' => $request->course,
        ]);

        return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student created successfully.');
    }

    public function show(string $id)
    {
        $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
        return view('students.show', compact('student'));
    }

    public function edit(string $id)
    {
        $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
        return view('students.edit', compact('student'));
    }

    public function update(Request $request, string $id)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'name'   => 'required',
            'email'  => 'required|email',
            'course' => 'required',
        ]);

        $student = Student::findOrFail($id);

        $student->update([
            'name'   => $request->name,
            'email'  => $request->email,
            'course' => $request->course,
        ]);

        return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student updated successfully.');
    }

    public function destroy(string $id)
    {
        $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
        $student->delete();

        return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student deleted successfully.');
    }
}
```

---

## 13. Understanding `index()` Method

```php
public function index()
{
    $students = Student::latest()->get();
    return view('students.index', compact('students'));
}
```

### কাজ কী?

- database থেকে সব student আনে
- latest অনুযায়ী order করে
- `students.index` view-এ পাঠায়

### কেন দরকার?

যখন আপনি student list page খুলবেন, তখন এই method call হবে।

---

## 14. Understanding `create()` Method

```php
public function create()
{
    return view('students.create');
}
```

### কাজ কী?

এটি শুধু form page return করে।

### কেন দরকার?

নতুন student add করার আগে user-কে একটি form দেখাতে হবে।

---

## 15. Understanding `store()` Method

```php
public function store(Request $request)
{
    $request->validate([
        'name'   => 'required',
        'email'  => 'required|email',
        'course' => 'required',
    ]);

    Student::create([
        'name'   => $request->name,
        'email'  => $request->email,
        'course' => $request->course,
    ]);

    return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student created successfully.');
}
```

### এখানে step by step কী হচ্ছে?

1. user form submit করেছে
2. request validation হচ্ছে
3. database-এ new student save হচ্ছে
4. তারপর list page-এ redirect করা হচ্ছে
5. success message পাঠানো হচ্ছে

### Important note

`Student::create()` use করতে model-এ `fillable` দিতে হবে।

---

## 16. Understanding `show()` Method

```php
public function show(string $id)
{
    $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
    return view('students.show', compact('student'));
}
```

### কাজ কী?

একটি specific student দেখায়।

### `findOrFail()` কেন?

- record পেলে return করবে
- না পেলে 404 error দিবে

এটি safer।

---

## 17. Understanding `edit()` Method

```php
public function edit(string $id)
{
    $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
    return view('students.edit', compact('student'));
}
```

### কাজ কী?

একটি specific student-এর existing data নিয়ে edit form দেখায়।

অর্থাৎ user যখন edit button-এ click করবে, তখন এই method call হবে।

---

## 18. Understanding `update()` Method

```php
public function update(Request $request, string $id)
{
    $request->validate([
        'name'   => 'required',
        'email'  => 'required|email',
        'course' => 'required',
    ]);

    $student = Student::findOrFail($id);

    $student->update([
        'name'   => $request->name,
        'email'  => $request->email,
        'course' => $request->course,
    ]);

    return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student updated successfully.');
}
```

### কাজ কী?

- edit form submit হওয়ার পর call হয়
- validation করে
- existing record update করে
- redirect করে

---

## 19. Understanding `destroy()` Method

```php
public function destroy(string $id)
{
    $student = Student::findOrFail($id);
    $student->delete();

    return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student deleted successfully.');
}
```

### কাজ কী?

নির্দিষ্ট student database থেকে delete করে।

---

## 20. Blade Views for CRUD

আমাদের কয়েকটি Blade file লাগবে:

```bash
resources/views/students/index.blade.php
resources/views/students/create.blade.php
resources/views/students/show.blade.php
resources/views/students/edit.blade.php
```

এখন এক এক করে দেখি।

---

## 21. Index View

```blade
<h1>All Students</h1>

<a href="{{ route('students.create') }}">Add New Student</a>

@if(session('success'))
    <p>{{ session('success') }}</p>
@endif

<table border="1" cellpadding="10">
    <tr>
        <th>ID</th>
        <th>Name</th>
        <th>Email</th>
        <th>Course</th>
        <th>Actions</th>
    </tr>

    @forelse($students as $student)
        <tr>
            <td>{{ $student->id }}</td>
            <td>{{ $student->name }}</td>
            <td>{{ $student->email }}</td>
            <td>{{ $student->course }}</td>
            <td>
                <a href="{{ route('students.show', $student->id) }}">View</a>
                <a href="{{ route('students.edit', $student->id) }}">Edit</a>

                <form action="{{ route('students.destroy', $student->id) }}" method="POST" style="display:inline;">
                    @csrf
                    @method('DELETE')
                    <button type="submit">Delete</button>
                </form>
            </td>
        </tr>
    @empty
        <tr>
            <td colspan="5">No students found.</td>
        </tr>
    @endforelse
</table>
```

### এখানে কী কী শিখলেন?

- `route()` helper
- `@forelse`
- `@csrf`
- `@method('DELETE')`

---

## 22. Create View

```blade
<h1>Create Student</h1>

<form action="{{ route('students.store') }}" method="POST">
    @csrf

    <div>
        <label>Name</label>
        <input type="text" name="name" value="{{ old('name') }}">
        @error('name')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <div>
        <label>Email</label>
        <input type="email" name="email" value="{{ old('email') }}">
        @error('email')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <div>
        <label>Course</label>
        <input type="text" name="course" value="{{ old('course') }}">
        @error('course')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <button type="submit">Save Student</button>
</form>
```

### এখানে important কী?

- `old()` দিয়ে আগের input দেখানো হচ্ছে
- `@error` দিয়ে validation error দেখানো হচ্ছে

---

## 23. Show View

```blade
<h1>Student Details</h1>

<p><strong>ID:</strong> {{ $student->id }}</p>
<p><strong>Name:</strong> {{ $student->name }}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> {{ $student->email }}</p>
<p><strong>Course:</strong> {{ $student->course }}</p>

<a href="{{ route('students.index') }}">Back</a>
```

এটি একটি student-এর details দেখায়।

---

## 24. Edit View

```blade
<h1>Edit Student</h1>

<form action="{{ route('students.update', $student->id) }}" method="POST">
    @csrf
    @method('PUT')

    <div>
        <label>Name</label>
        <input type="text" name="name" value="{{ old('name', $student->name) }}">
        @error('name')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <div>
        <label>Email</label>
        <input type="email" name="email" value="{{ old('email', $student->email) }}">
        @error('email')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <div>
        <label>Course</label>
        <input type="text" name="course" value="{{ old('course', $student->course) }}">
        @error('course')
            <p>{{ $message }}</p>
        @enderror
    </div>

    <button type="submit">Update Student</button>
</form>
```

### এখানে `old('name', $student->name)` কেন?

- validation fail হলে old value দেখাবে
- না হলে existing database value দেখাবে

---

## 25. Form Validation

`store()` এবং `update()` method-এ validation use করা হয়েছে।

```php
$request->validate([
    'name'   => 'required',
    'email'  => 'required|email',
    'course' => 'required',
]);
```

### এর মানে:

- `name` অবশ্যই দিতে হবে
- `email` অবশ্যই valid email হতে হবে
- `course` অবশ্যই দিতে হবে

এতে invalid data save হওয়া কমে যায়।

---

## 26. PUT, PATCH, DELETE and Blade Forms

HTML form সরাসরি `PUT`, `PATCH`, `DELETE` support করে না।
তাই Laravel এ method spoofing ব্যবহার করা হয়।

### Update form

```blade
<form action="{{ route('students.update', $student->id) }}" method="POST">
    @csrf
    @method('PUT')
</form>
```

### Delete form

```blade
<form action="{{ route('students.destroy', $student->id) }}" method="POST">
    @csrf
    @method('DELETE')
</form>
```

এভাবে Laravel বুঝে নেয় আসল request method কী।

---

## 27. Redirect with Success Message

Controller-এ:

```php
return redirect()->route('students.index')->with('success', 'Student created successfully.');
```

### এখানে:

- `redirect()` → অন্য page-এ পাঠায়
- `route('students.index')` → index route-এ যায়
- `with('success', ...)` → session flash message পাঠায়

---

## 28. Displaying Flash Messages

Blade file-এ success message দেখাতে পারেন:

```blade
@if(session('success'))
    <p>{{ session('success') }}</p>
@endif
```

### কাজ কী?

যদি session-এ success message থাকে, তাহলে দেখাবে।

---

## 29. Real-Life Flow of Resource Controller

ধরি CodeJogot-এর dashboard-এ student manage করছেন। 😊

### Full flow:

1. Admin `/students` এ যায় → `index()`
2. “Add New Student” এ click করে → `create()`
3. Form submit করে → `store()`
4. Student list-এ ফিরে আসে
5. “View” click করে → `show()`
6. “Edit” click করে → `edit()`
7. Edit form submit করে → `update()`
8. “Delete” click করে → `destroy()`

অর্থাৎ একটি resource-এর পুরো lifecycle এই controller handle করে।

---

## 30. Best Practices

### 1. Model-এ `fillable` ব্যবহার করুন

`Student::create()` এবং `$student->update()` use করতে model-এ fillable দিতে হবে।

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class Student extends Model
{
    protected $fillable = ['name', 'email', 'course'];
}
```

না দিলে mass assignment error আসতে পারে।

---

### 2. `findOrFail()` ব্যবহার করুন

```php
$student = Student::findOrFail($id);
```

এটি record না পেলে automatically 404 দেয়। safer approach।

---

### 3. Validation সবসময় দিন

বিশেষ করে `store()` এবং `update()` method-এ।

---

### 4. Views আলাদা রাখুন

- `index.blade.php`
- `create.blade.php`
- `show.blade.php`
- `edit.blade.php`

এতে maintain সহজ হয়।

---

### 5. Route name ব্যবহার করুন

hard-coded URL না লিখে:

```blade
route('students.index')
route('students.store')
route('students.edit', $student->id)
```

এতে route change হলেও code কম break হয়।

---

### 6. Controller slim রাখুন

খুব complex business logic অন্য class-এ সরিয়ে দিন, controller-এ শুধু request/response flow রাখুন।

---

## 31. Summary

Laravel Resource Controller হলো CRUD operation organize করার standard এবং powerful উপায়। ✅

### Main methods এক নজরে

```php
index()
create()
store()
show()
edit()
update()
destroy()
```

### Main resource route

```php
Route::resource('students', StudentController::class);
```

### Resource controller-এর benefits

- less code
- standard structure
- clean routes
- easier maintenance
- Laravel convention follow

---

## ছোট্ট Final Example

### Route

```php
use App\Http\Controllers\StudentController;

Route::resource('students', StudentController::class);
```

### Controller

```php
public function index()
{
    $students = Student::all();
    return view('students.index', compact('students'));
}
```

### View

```blade
@foreach($students as $student)
    <p>{{ $student->name }}</p>
@endforeach
```

এখানে route controller call করছে, controller database থেকে data আনছে, আর Blade view data দেখাচ্ছে। এটাই Resource Controller-এর core workflow। 🎉

</div>

আমরা এখানে একটি **Student Management System** বানাবো, যেখানে থাকবে:

- Student List

- Delete Student
- Tailwind CSS Design

## 1. Project Overview

এই project এ আমরা একটি **Student CRUD Application** বানাবো।

CRUD মানে:

- **C** = Create
- **R** = Read
- **U** = Update
- **D** = Delete

অর্থাৎ, আমরা student data:

- add করতে পারবো
- list আকারে দেখতে পারবো
- edit করতে পারবো
- delete করতে পারবো

---

## 2. What We Will Build

এই project এ একটি student-এর জন্য নিচের fields থাকবে:

- Name
- Email
- Course

আমরা সুন্দরভাবে Tailwind CSS দিয়ে UI বানাবো।

---

## 3. Project Setup

প্রথমে Laravel project create করুন:

```bash
composer create-project laravel/laravel student-crud
```

তারপর project folder এ যান:

```bash
cd student-crud
```

## 4. Database Configuration

`.env` file open করুন এবং database config ঠিক করুন:

```env
DB_CONNECTION=mysql
DB_HOST=127.0.0.1
DB_PORT=3306
DB_DATABASE=student_crud
DB_USERNAME=root
DB_PASSWORD=
```

তারপর আপনার MySQL-এ `student_crud` নামে database create করুন।

## 5. Install Tailwind CSS

Laravel-এর সাথে Vite থাকে, তাই Tailwind install করা সহজ।

Command run করুন:

```bash
npm install
npm install -D tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite
```

এখন `vite.config.js` file update করুন:

```js
import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import laravel from "laravel-vite-plugin";
import tailwindcss from "@tailwindcss/vite";

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [
    laravel({
      input: ["resources/css/app.css", "resources/js/app.js"],
      refresh: true,
    }),
    tailwindcss(),
  ],
});
```

এখন `resources/css/app.css` file এ লিখুন:

```css
@import "tailwindcss";
```

---

## 6. Create Model, Migration, Controller

এখন এক command এ সব create করি:

```bash
php artisan make:model Student -mcr
```

এখানে:

- `-m` = migration
- `-c` = controller
- `-r` = resource controller

---

## 7. Migration Code

এখন migration file open করুন:

```php
use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('students', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->string('name');
            $table->string('email');
            $table->string('course');
            $table->timestamps();
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('students');
    }
};
```

তারপর migrate চালান:

```bash
php artisan migrate
```

---

## 8. Student Model Setup

`app/Models/Student.php` file এ লিখুন:

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class Student extends Model
{
    protected $fillable = ['name', 'email', 'course'];
}
```

### কেন `fillable` দরকার?

কারণ আমরা `create()` এবং `update()` method ব্যবহার করবো।
`fillable` না দিলে Laravel mass assignment error দিতে পারে।

---

## 9. Resource Route Setup

`routes/web.php` file এ লিখুন:

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route;
use App\Http\Controllers\StudentController;

Route::get('/', function () {
    return redirect()->route('students.index');
});

Route::resource('students', StudentController::class);
```

---

## 10. Controller Full Code

এখন `app/Http/Controllers/StudentController.php` file এ full code লিখুন:

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use App\Models\Student;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class StudentController extends Controller
{
    public function index()
    {
        $students = Student::latest()->get();
        return view('students.index', compact('students'));
    }

    public function create()
    {
        return view('students.create');
    }

    public function store(Request $request)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'name'   => 'required|string|max:255',
            'email'  => 'required|email|max:255',
            'course' => 'required|string|max:255',
        ]);

        Student::create([
            'name'   => $request->name,
            'email'  => $request->email,
            'course' => $request->course,
        ]);

        return redirect()->route('students.index')
            ->with('success', 'Student created successfully.');
    }

    public function show(Student $student)
    {
        return view('students.show', compact('student'));
    }

    public function edit(Student $student)
    {
        return view('students.edit', compact('student'));
    }

    public function update(Request $request, Student $student)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'name'   => 'required|string|max:255',
            'email'  => 'required|email|max:255',
            'course' => 'required|string|max:255',
        ]);

        $student->update([
            'name'   => $request->name,
            'email'  => $request->email,
            'course' => $request->course,
        ]);

        return redirect()->route('students.index')
            ->with('success', 'Student updated successfully.');
    }

    public function destroy(Student $student)
    {
        $student->delete();

        return redirect()->route('students.index')
            ->with('success', 'Student deleted successfully.');
    }
}
```

---

## 12. Create Index Page

এখন list page বানাই।

`resources/views/students/index.blade.php`

```blade
@extends('layouts.app')

@section('content')
    <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
        <h2 class="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-800">All Students</h2>
        <a href="{{ route('students.create') }}"
           class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white px-5 py-2 rounded-lg shadow">
            + Add Student
        </a>
    </div>

    <div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md overflow-hidden">
        <table class="w-full text-left">
            <thead class="bg-gray-200">
                <tr>
                    <th class="px-6 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700">#</th>
                    <th class="px-6 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700">Name</th>
                    <th class="px-6 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700">Email</th>
                    <th class="px-6 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700">Course</th>
                    <th class="px-6 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700">Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                @forelse($students as $student)
                    <tr class="border-t hover:bg-gray-50">
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">{{ $loop->iteration }}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">{{ $student->name }}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">{{ $student->email }}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">{{ $student->course }}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">
                            <div class="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
                                <a href="{{ route('students.show', $student->id) }}"
                                   class="bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded-md text-sm">
                                    View
                                </a>

                                <a href="{{ route('students.edit', $student->id) }}"
                                   class="bg-yellow-500 hover:bg-yellow-600 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded-md text-sm">
                                    Edit
                                </a>

                                <form action="{{ route('students.destroy', $student->id) }}" method="POST"
                                      onsubmit="return confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this student?')">
                                    @csrf
                                    @method('DELETE')
                                    <button type="submit"
                                            class="bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded-md text-sm">
                                        Delete
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            </div>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                @empty
                    <tr>
                        <td colspan="5" class="px-6 py-6 text-center text-gray-500">
                            No students found.
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                @endforelse
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>
@endsection
```

## 13. Create Create Page

`resources/views/students/create.blade.php`

```blade
@extends('layouts.app')

@section('content')
    <div class="max-w-2xl mx-auto bg-white p-8 rounded-xl shadow-md">
        <h2 class="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6">Add New Student</h2>

        <form action="{{ route('students.store') }}" method="POST" class="space-y-5">
            @csrf

            <div>
                <label class="block text-gray-700 font-medium mb-2">Name</label>
                <input type="text" name="name" value="{{ old('name') }}"
                       class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                @error('name')
                    <p class="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{{ $message }}</p>
                @enderror
            </div>

            <div>
                <label class="block text-gray-700 font-medium mb-2">Email</label>
                <input type="email" name="email" value="{{ old('email') }}"
                       class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                @error('email')
                    <p class="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{{ $message }}</p>
                @enderror
            </div>

            <div>
                <label class="block text-gray-700 font-medium mb-2">Course</label>
                <input type="text" name="course" value="{{ old('course') }}"
                       class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                @error('course')
                    <p class="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{{ $message }}</p>
                @enderror
            </div>

            <div class="flex gap-3">
                <button type="submit"
                        class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white px-5 py-2 rounded-lg shadow">
                    Save Student
                </button>

                <a href="{{ route('students.index') }}"
                   class="bg-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-600 text-white px-5 py-2 rounded-lg shadow">
                    Back
                </a>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
@endsection
```

## 17. Full Project Flow

এখন project এ যা হবে:

### 1. Home page

`/` এ গেলে automatically `students.index` page-এ redirect হবে।

### 2. Add Student

“Add Student” button click করলে create form আসবে।

### 3. Save Student

Form submit করলে database-এ data save হবে।

### 4. View Student

List থেকে View button click করলে specific student details দেখাবে।

### 5. Edit Student

Edit button click করলে student-এর আগের data form-এ দেখাবে।

### 6. Update Student

Update করলে database-এ data change হবে।

### 7. Delete Student

Delete button click করলে student remove হয়ে যাবে।

---

## 18. File Structure

এই project এ প্রধান file structure হবে এমন:

```bash
app/
 └── Http/
      └── Controllers/
           └── StudentController.php

app/
 └── Models/
      └── Student.php

database/
 └── migrations/
      └── xxxx_xx_xx_create_students_table.php

resources/
 └── views/
      ├── layouts/
      │    └── app.blade.php
      └── students/
           ├── index.blade.php
           ├── create.blade.php
           ├── edit.blade.php
           └── show.blade.php

routes/
 └── web.php
```

---

## 19. How Each Part Works

### Controller

সব request handle করে।

### Model

database এর `students` table এর সাথে কাজ করে।

### Migration

database table structure define করে।

### Route

URL এবং controller method connect করে।

### Blade View

frontend UI দেখায়।

### Tailwind CSS

design সুন্দর করে।

---

## 20. Final Result

এই project complete হলে আপনি একটি সুন্দর Tailwind CSS based CRUD application পাবেন যেখানে:

- modern UI থাকবে
- validation থাকবে
- success message থাকবে
- update এবং delete properly কাজ করবে
- Laravel Resource Controller pattern follow করা হবে

---

# Important Extra Note

## Route Model Binding কেন ভালো?

আমি controller এ এটা ব্যবহার করেছি:

```php
public function edit(Student $student)
```

এটা Laravel-এর **Route Model Binding**।
এর মানে হলো, URL থেকে student id নিয়ে Laravel automatically সেই student record খুঁজে এনে `$student` variable-এ দিয়ে দেয়।

এই approach beginner-friendly এবং clean।

---

# Bonus: Common Commands

```bash
composer create-project laravel/laravel student-crud
cd student-crud
npm install
npm install -D tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite
php artisan make:model Student -mcr
php artisan migrate
php artisan serve
npm run dev
```

# Project 02: Student Teacher Role Based Auth

## ✅ Step 1: Laravel Project Setup

```bash
composer create-project laravel/laravel role-based-auth
cd role-based-auth
```

---

## ✅ Step 2: Install Laravel Breeze

```bash
composer require laravel/breeze --dev
php artisan breeze:install
npm install && npm run dev
php artisan migrate
```

> এখন আপনি Login/Register UI পাবেন `/login` এবং `/register` এ।

---

## ✅ Step 3: Add `role` Column to Users Table

Migration File এডিট করুন:

```bash
php artisan make:migration add_role_column_to_users_table --table=users
```

**database/migrations/xxxx_xx_xx_add_role_column_to_users_table.php**

```php
public function up()
{
    Schema::table('users', function (Blueprint $table) {
        $table->string('role')->default('student'); // student, teacher
    });
}
```

তারপর:

```bash
php artisan migrate
```

---

## ✅ Step 4: Update Register Form with Role Selection

### ✅ A. Edit Blade View

**resources/views/auth/register.blade.php**

নিচের কোডটি ফর্মে যোগ করুন:

```html
<div>
  <x-input-label for="role" :value="__('Role')" />
  <select
    id="role"
    name="role"
    class="block mt-1 w-full border-gray-300 focus:border-indigo-500 focus:ring-indigo-500 rounded-md shadow-sm"
  >
    <option value="student">Student</option>
    <option value="teacher">Teacher</option>
  </select>
  <x-input-error :messages="$errors->get('role')" class="mt-2" />
</div>
```

### ✅ B. Update Register Request Validation

**app/Http/Controllers/Auth/RegisteredUserController.php**

```php
use Illuminate\Validation\Rules;

public function store(Request $request)
{
    $request->validate([
        'name' => ['required', 'string', 'max:255'],
        'email' => ['required', 'string', 'lowercase', 'email', 'max:255', 'unique:'.User::class],
        'password' => ['required', 'confirmed', Rules\Password::defaults()],
        'role' => ['required', 'in:student,teacher'],
    ]);

    $user = User::create([
        'name' => $request->name,
        'email' => $request->email,
        'password' => Hash::make($request->password),
        'role' => $request->role,
    ]);

    event(new Registered($user));

    Auth::login($user);

    return redirect(RouteServiceProvider::HOME);
}
```

---

## ✅ Step 5: Redirect Based on Role

**app/Providers/RouteServiceProvider.php**

```php
public const HOME = '/dashboard';
```

এখন ডাশবোর্ডের জন্য Route & Controller তৈরি করুন।

---

## ✅ Step 6: Create Dashboard Routes & Views

**routes/web.php**

```php
use App\Http\Controllers\DashboardController;

Route::middleware(['auth'])->group(function () {
    Route::get('/dashboard', [DashboardController::class, 'index'])->name('dashboard');
});
```

**Create Controller:**

```bash
php artisan make:controller DashboardController
```

**app/Http/Controllers/DashboardController.php**

```php
namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class DashboardController extends Controller
{
    public function index()
    {
        if (auth()->user()->role === 'teacher') {
            return view('dashboard.teacher');
        } else {
            return view('dashboard.student');
        }
    }
}
```

---

## ✅ Step 7: Create Role-Based Views

**resources/views/dashboard/student.blade.php**

```blade
<x-app-layout>
    <x-slot name="header">
        <h2 class="font-semibold text-xl text-gray-800 leading-tight">Student Dashboard</h2>
    </x-slot>

    <div class="py-12">
        <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
            <div class="bg-white overflow-hidden shadow-sm sm:rounded-lg">
                <div class="p-6 text-gray-900">Welcome Student!</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</x-app-layout>
```

**resources/views/dashboard/teacher.blade.php**

```blade
<x-app-layout>
    <x-slot name="header">
        <h2 class="font-semibold text-xl text-gray-800 leading-tight">Teacher Dashboard</h2>
    </x-slot>

    <div class="py-12">
        <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
            <div class="bg-white overflow-hidden shadow-sm sm:rounded-lg">
                <div class="p-6 text-gray-900">Welcome Teacher!</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</x-app-layout>
```

---

## ✅ Step 8: (Optional) Middleware for Role Restriction

চাইলে আপনি রোলের উপর ভিত্তি করে Middleware তৈরি করতে পারেন।

```bash
php artisan make:middleware EnsureUserIsTeacher
```

**EnsureUserIsTeacher.php**

```php
public function handle($request, Closure $next)
{
    if (auth()->check() && auth()->user()->role !== 'teacher') {
        return redirect()->route('dashboard');
    }

    return $next($request);
}
```

Register করুন: `app/Http/Kernel.php` -> `$routeMiddleware` এ যোগ করুন:

```php
'teacher' => \App\Http\Middleware\EnsureUserIsTeacher::class,
```

এখন কোনো route এ শুধুমাত্র টিচার দেখতে পারবে:

```php
Route::get('/teacher-only', function () {
    return "Only Teachers Can See This!";
})->middleware('teacher');
```

---

## ✅ Step 9: Test the Application

1. Register করুন → Role নির্বাচন করুন (Student or Teacher)
2. Login করুন
3. Role অনুযায়ী ভিন্ন ড্যাশবোর্ড দেখুন
